    5014                 :            : /*                                                                      */
    5015                 :            : /*      Convert mapserver regex expression to ogc is like propoery      */
    5016                 :            : /*      exprssion.                                                      */
    5017                 :            : /*                                                                      */
    5018                 :            : /*      Review bug 1644 for details. Here are the current rules:        */
    5019                 :            : /*                                                                      */
    5020                 :            : /*       The filter encoding property like is more limited compared     */
    5021                 :            : /*      to regular expressiosn that can be built in mapserver. I        */
    5022                 :            : /*      think we should define what is possible to convert properly     */
    5023                 :            : /*      and do those, and also identify potential problems.  Example :  */
    5024                 :            : /*        - any time there is a .* in the expression it will be         */
    5025                 :            : /*      converted to *                                                  */
    5026                 :            : /*        - any other character plus all the metacharcters . ^ $ * +    */
    5027                 :            : /*      ? { [ ] \ | ( ) would be outputed as is. (In case of            */
    5028                 :            : /*      mapserver, when we read the the ogc filter expression, we       */
    5029                 :            : /*      convert the wild card chracter to .*, and we convert the        */
    5030                 :            : /*      single chracter to .  and the escpae character to \ all         */
    5031                 :            : /*      other are outputed as is)                                       */
    5032                 :            : /*        - the  ogc tag would look like <ogc:PropertyIsLike            */
    5033                 :            : /*      wildCard="*"  singleChar="." escape="\">                        */
    5034                 :            : /*                                                                      */
    5035                 :            : /*        - type of potential problem :                                 */
    5036                 :            : /*           * if an expression is like /T (star)/ it will be           */
    5037                 :            : /*      converted to T* which is not correct.                           */
    5038                 :            : /*                                                                      */
